<html><head></head><body><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: auto ease 0s 1 normal none running none; padding-top: 30px; position: relative; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">are envy and jealousy similar psychologically</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span>While often used interchangeably in casual conversation,&nbsp;</span><mark style="border-radius: 4px; background-image: ; background-position-x: ; background-position-y: ; background-size: ; background-repeat: ; background-attachment: ; background-origin: ; background-clip: ; padding: 0px 2px;">envy and jealousy are psychologically distinct emotions with different origins and dynamics</mark>.&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Envy</span>&nbsp;is the desire for something someone else possesses (a two-person dynamic), whereas&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">jealousy</span>&nbsp;is the fear of losing something you already have to a third party (a three-person dynamic).<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 102.359px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Verywell Mind</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Key Psychological Distinctions<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Social Dynamic:</span></span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Envy (Two-party):</span>&nbsp;Typically involves just you and the person who has what you want, such as their success, physical traits, or possessions.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Jealousy (Three-party):</span>&nbsp;Almost always involves a "rivalry triangle" consisting of you, someone you value (like a partner), and a third party perceived as a threat.</span></li></ul></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Root Cause and Emotional Tone:</span></span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Envy:</span>&nbsp;Stemming from&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">comparison</span>, it often triggers feelings of inferiority, longing, and resentment. It can be&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">benign</span>&nbsp;(motivating self-improvement) or&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">malicious</span>&nbsp;(desiring that the other person loses what they have).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Jealousy:</span>&nbsp;Rooted in&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">attachment insecurity</span>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">fear of loss</span>, it is characterized by anxiety, suspicion, anger, and protectiveness.</span></li></ul></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Biological Link:</span></span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Both emotions are considered transformations of&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">shame</span>, occurring when you measure yourself against others and feel you fall short or are at risk of being replaced.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 122.547px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; While commonly associated with romantic affairs, this third party can be&nbsp;<mark style="border-radius: 4px; background-image: ; background-position-x: ; background-position-y: ; background-size: ; background-repeat: ; background-attachment: ; background-origin: ; background-clip: ; padding: 0px 2px;">anyone—or anything—that is perceived as a threat to the stability or exclusivity of a valued bond</mark>.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 80.6406px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Wikipedia</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Psychologically, the third party represents an interruption to your connection with a "valued other". Common examples include:<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 123.805px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">What is Compersion?</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Social and Personal Contexts<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Romantic Rivals:</span>&nbsp;A new person your partner is flirting with, an ex-partner, or even a friend who seems to be receiving "too much" of your partner's emotional intimacy.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">New Siblings:</span>&nbsp;In family dynamics, a newborn baby is a classic "third party" that threatens a child's exclusive access to a parent's attention and resources.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">New Friends:</span>&nbsp;In platonic relationships, jealousy can arise when a close friend makes a new friend, triggering a fear of being "replaced" in the social hierarchy.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 81.3906px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Wikipedia</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Professional Contexts<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Coworkers:</span>&nbsp;A colleague who receives the praise, mentorship, or promotion you feel entitled to can be viewed as a rival.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Supervisors:</span>&nbsp;In cases of&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">triangulation</span>, a boss might be the third party that disrupts the bond between team members, or conversely, a coworker might threaten your specific relationship with a supervisor.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 102.539px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Non-Human "Third Parties"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Interestingly, the third party does not always have to be a person. It can be an&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">imaginary figure</span>&nbsp;created by anxiety or even a time-consuming hobby or career that "steals" a person's attention away from the relationship.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 138.547px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Structure:</span>&nbsp;This is a two-person dynamic:&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">You</span>&nbsp;and the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Target</span>&nbsp;who has the thing you lack.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Driver:</span>&nbsp;It is driven by&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">social comparison</span>, not a threat to a relationship.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 102.539px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Verywell Mind</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Can you feel "jealousy" toward them?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Psychologically, you cannot strictly feel&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">jealousy</em>&nbsp;toward a trait or possession because jealousy requires a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">fear of loss</span>.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 55.6562px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Calm</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">You don't "lose" your own success because someone else is successful.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">However, if you feel that a coworker’s success will cause you to&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">lose your status</span>&nbsp;or your boss's favor, that fear of losing your "territory" to them&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">is</em>&nbsp;jealousy.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 98.7031px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Mike Robbins</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Hate without a "Perceived Threat"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Yes, you can feel hatred or extreme resentment without a direct threat. This is often called&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">malicious envy</span>.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 68.0703px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">ReachLink</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Malicious Envy:</span>&nbsp;You don't just want the success or trait; you want the other person to&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">lose it</span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Root Cause:</span>&nbsp;This often stems from a deep sense of perceived unfairness or the feeling that someone else's gain highlights your own perceived failure. The "hate" is a defense mechanism to protect your own ego from feeling "less than".</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 64.4688px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; 0;">&nbsp;+5</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div style="overflow-x: auto; margin-block: 16px 24px; box-sizing: border-box; scrollbar-width: none; inline-size: calc(100% + 20px); They are both considered negative emotional states characterized by similar levels of negative affect and psychological distress.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Feelings of Inferiority:</span>&nbsp;At their center, both involve a painful awareness of lacking something—be it success, a trait, or a possession—that someone else has.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Functional Goal:</span>&nbsp;Psychologically, both serve to "level the gap" between you and the person you are comparing yourself to, though they use opposite methods to achieve this.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 179.391px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PubMed Central (PMC) (.gov)</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Key Differences<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The primary distinction lies in whether the emotion motivates you to&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">"level up"</span>&nbsp;(benign) or&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">"pull down"</span>&nbsp;(malicious).<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 120.766px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 16px 8px 0px; text-align: left;">Feature<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Benign Envy</span>&nbsp;is primarily characterized by negative emotion&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">toward the self</span>, manifesting as impatience or a loss of confidence because you haven't yet reached a desired standard.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Malicious Envy</span>&nbsp;is defined by negative emotion&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">toward the envied person</span>, involving frustration, irritation, and a sense that the other's success is unfair.</span></li></ul></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Motivational Outcomes:</span></span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Benign Envy</span>&nbsp;triggers a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">"leveling up"</span>&nbsp;motivation. It inspires self-improvement, emulation, and higher goal-setting.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Malicious Envy</span>&nbsp;triggers a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">"leveling down"</span>&nbsp;motivation. The goal is to damage the other's position or revel in their misfortune (<em style="font-weight: inherit;">schadenfreude</em>).</span></li></ul></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Personality Links:</span>&nbsp;Both forms correlate with&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Machiavellianism</span>&nbsp;(using strategic tactics to gain status), but malicious envy is uniquely linked to&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">psychopathy</span>&nbsp;and a desire for social conflict.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 123.094px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Hogrefe eContent</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+6</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div style="overflow-x: auto; margin-block: 16px 24px; box-sizing: border-box; scrollbar-width: none; inline-size: calc(100% + 20px); <html><head></head><body><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div style="color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"></div><div style="color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span>Envy is a painful, self-conscious emotion triggered by an "upward social comparison"—when someone else has a quality, achievement, or possession you lack</span>. Psychologically,&nbsp;<mark style="border-radius: 4px; background-image: ; background-position-x: ; background-position-y: ; background-size: ; background-repeat: ; background-attachment: ; background-origin: ; background-clip: ; padding: 0px 2px;">it functions as an alarm system that signals a threat to your social status or self-view</mark>.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 58.7266px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Wiley</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Whether this envy becomes&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">benign</span>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">malicious</span>&nbsp;depends on how you "appraise" or interpret the situation:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Benign envy is a frustrating but constructive force. It focuses on the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">self</span>&nbsp;and how to improve your own position.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 122.125px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Psychology Today</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Key Triggers:</span>&nbsp;You perceive the other person's success as&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">deserved</span>&nbsp;(earned through effort) and believe the goal is&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">attainable</span>&nbsp;for you (high control potential).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Core Emotion:</span>&nbsp;Negative emotion directed toward the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">self</span>&nbsp;(e.g., feeling inadequate or impatient).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Psychological Function:</span>&nbsp;It acts as a motivator to "level up" and close the gap through hard work, emulation, and self-improvement.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 179.688px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Malicious Envy ("Pulling Down")<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Malicious envy is a hostile and toxic force. It focuses on the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">other person</span>&nbsp;and a desire to see them lose their advantage.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 149.523px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Georgetown University</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Key Triggers:</span>&nbsp;You perceive the other person's success as&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">undeserved</span>&nbsp;(due to luck or unfairness) and feel you have&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">no control</span>&nbsp;over achieving it yourself.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Core Emotion:</span>&nbsp;Negative emotion directed toward the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">other person</span>&nbsp;(e.g., resentment, hostility, or ill will).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Psychological Function:</span>&nbsp;It attempts to "level down" the status gap by undermining or sabotaging the superior person. It is often associated with&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">schadenfreude</em>&nbsp;(taking joy in the other's misfortune).</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: <html><head></head><body><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: auto ease 0s 1 normal none running none; padding-top: 30px; position: relative; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span>Psychologically, schadenfreude—the pleasure derived from another's misfortune—is a complex but universal human emotion rooted in&nbsp;</span><span style="font-weight: 700;">social comparison</span>,&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">justice</span>, and&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">group identity</span>. padding: 0px 2px;">typically functions as a reward response in the brain when a setback to another person benefits our own sense of status or fairness</mark>.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Boost to Self-Esteem:</span>&nbsp;When someone we perceive as superior or more successful fails, it reduces the "status gap" between us, making us feel more adequate.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Deserved Punishment:</span>&nbsp;If someone is seen as arrogant, hypocritical, or has acted unfairly, their misfortune is perceived as a "comeuppance" or "karma".</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 140.797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">All About Psychology</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; Group Identity (Rivalry &amp; Aggression)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Schadenfreude often arises in the context of "us vs. them" dynamics.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 180.836px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PubMed Central (PMC) (.gov)</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">In-Group Bonding:</span>&nbsp;Sharing joy in a rival's failure (like a sports team or political opponent) strengthens the bonds within one's own group.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Dehumanization:</span>&nbsp;In extreme cases, we may view members of an "out-group" as less human, which suppresses our natural empathy and allows pleasure to take its place.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 84.1641px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Britannica</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">4. Compensation<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Sometimes, we feel pleasure because another person’s failure mirrors our own previous failures.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 167.531px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PubMed Central (PMC) (.gov)</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Validation:</span>&nbsp;Knowing that others also suffer setbacks makes us feel less alone or "uniquely incompetent" in our own misfortunes.</span><span><span style="position: relative; min-width: 0px;">Psychology Today</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; Activity:</span>&nbsp;Neuroscience shows that schadenfreude activates the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">ventral striatum</span>, a part of the brain's reward system also triggered by personal success.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Early Onset:</span>&nbsp;The emotion is not learned later in life; it has been observed in children as young as&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">24 months old</span>, particularly when they see a "misbehaving" peer or sibling get into trouble.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span>Social Networking Services (SNS) significantly amplify schadenfreude by creating "affective infrastructures" that prioritize high-arousal emotions and social comparison</span>. These platforms transform a historically private emotion into a public, performative act through features like reaction buttons and viral comment sections.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 132.445px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Lampoon Magazine</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Mechanisms of Amplification<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Social Comparison &amp; Status Re-evaluation</span>: Constant exposure to others' idealized "curated highs" fuels envy and upward comparison. When these successful individuals suffer a setback, users experience&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Compensation Schadenfreude</span>, a relief that reduces their own feelings of inferiority and restores self-image.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Anonymity &amp; Deindividuation</span>: The relative anonymity of SNS lowers social barriers and reduces the perceived consequences of expressing "malicious joy". In large online groups, individuals may experience&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">deindividuation</span>, feeling less personal responsibility for their comments, which intensifies schadenfreudian behavior like mocking celebrities or rivals.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Algorithmic Reinforcement</span>: Platforms use engagement-driven ranking that privileges content provoking strong reactions. When a public failure or scandal goes viral, the algorithm creates a "feedback loop of reward," validating the observer's satisfaction and encouraging further sharing.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Partisan Polarization</span>: Social media serves as a gateway for political news where users primarily encounter content aligned with their in-group. This&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">affective polarization</span>&nbsp;makes it more likely that the misfortunes of political adversaries ("out-groups") are met with gratification rather than empathy.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 77.4688px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Frontiers</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+9</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Psychological &amp; Social Impact<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Mental Health Consequences</span>: While schadenfreude offers momentary pleasure, constant exposure to others' misfortunes can lead to a culture of negativity and&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">empathy fatigue</span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Schadenfreude-Induced Anxiety</span>: Witnessing a peer's failure (like a tech layoff or public "callout") can trigger a "body alarm" in observers, leading to fears that they might be next.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Erosion of Trust</span>: Widespread celebration of others' struggles can toxicify the digital environment, eroding social cohesion and trust within communities.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Bipartisan Lawmakers</span>: Support for bills like the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://now.org/media-center/press-release/pass-the-kids-off-social-media-act/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">Kids Off Social Media Act</a></span>&nbsp;is rare for its bipartisan nature, with strong backing from both Republicans (73%) and Democrats (56%).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Victim Advocacy Groups</span>: Groups like the Social Media Victims Law Center and the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.socialmediasafety.org/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; Real-World Application &amp; Workarounds</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Historically, "self-certification" (just typing a birthdate) was the standard, and it was easily bypassed. However, new laws—like those in&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><div style="display: inline;"><a tabindex="0" role="button" href="https://www.google.com/search?q=australia&amp;kgmid=%2Fm%2F0chghy&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=2ahUKEwjesdzv1uCTAxV-LkQIHQoUC5EQ3egRegYIAQgEEAI&amp;gl=us" style="text-decoration-thickness: 10%; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 53.6172px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Technological Barriers</span>: Major platforms are increasingly using&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">AI-powered age estimation</span>&nbsp;(analyzing facial features via video selfies) or requiring&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">government ID</span>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">credit card</span>&nbsp;checks.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Circumvention</span>: While kids still try tricks like using VPNs, wearing makeup to look older, or using parents' accounts, platforms like Meta and TikTok have deactivated hundreds of thousands of accounts in 2026 to avoid massive fines (up to $32M in Australia).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The "VPN Problem"</span>: In regions where adult content or social media is age-gated, there has been a massive spike in VPN usage to route around local restrictions.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 54.2734px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">BBC</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">2. Role of Parental Approval</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Parental consent does change the legal and functional landscape, but it varies by region.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The "13 to 15" Bracket</span>: In many jurisdictions (like the EU and several U.S. states), children aged 13-15 can access platforms&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">only with verifiable parental consent</span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Data Protection</span>: Laws like&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">COPPA</span>&nbsp;(U.S.) and&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">GDPR</span>&nbsp;(EU) require platforms to get parent permission before collecting data on minors. If a parent "vouchers" for a child, the platform's liability is reduced.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Access vs. Safety</span>: Even with consent, some new laws (like New York’s&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">SAFE for Kids Act</span>) still restrict "addictive feeds" and late-night notifications for anyone under 18.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 129.875px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Study International</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">3. Tech Freedom: Mastodon &amp; Self-Hosted Platforms</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The legal landscape for decentralized or small-scale platforms is currently a "grey area."<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Targeted Enforcement</span>: Most current laws (like Australia's under-16 ban) specifically target&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">"high-risk platforms"</span>&nbsp;or those with a large commercial benefit. Non-profits, educational sites, and smaller niche platforms are often exempted.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Resource Constraints</span>: Self-hosted instances or decentralized networks like Mastodon often lack the budget to implement the expensive age-verification systems (like those from&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Yoti</span>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">LexisNexis</span>) that regulators now expect from "Big Tech".</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Safety Trade-offs</span>: While these platforms offer more freedom, they also lack the sophisticated automated moderation and reporting tools found on major SNS, which can actually make them more dangerous for minors if they are not actively moderated.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 54.2734px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">BBC</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; risks</span>&nbsp;of providing biometric data for age verification, or how to set up&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">family sharing</span>&nbsp;tools to manage these approvals?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg
